It was almost five o'clock in the afternoon when I checked in. The lobby manager took the initiative to add WeChat. The service was very considerate. If you need anything, you will arrange for the waiter to deliver it immediately. It feels like home. Afternoon tea ended at 4:30 and I didn't catch it. In the evening, I helped to pack and deliver it to the room. There were coffee, black tea, cakes, cookies, and fruit platters, which were pretty good. Let's talk about the room. I like this balcony very much. Looking at the fog on the mountain, the air is very fresh. The room is well soundproofed. It is very quiet at night, not noisy at all, and the mattress is soft and comfortable. The buffet breakfast tastes very good, the chef's skills are good, and there are many varieties. After breakfast, go to the temple opposite to burn incense and worship Buddha. There is no entrance fee. You can scan the code to buy incense and candles by yourself. There is no management. Everyone is conscious and the folk customs are simple. Finally, let me talk about the hot springs. The aunt in the bathroom was very friendly. The water temperature of the hot springs was about 40 degrees, not cold or hot, but I have to complain that there were too few open pools. I saw a sign saying that 16 pools were available today, but there was no detailed count. The pools were very small, and basically two or three people occupied one pit. I went around and soaked in three pools, two Chinese medicine pools and one original soup pool. The water was a bit turbid and slippery, and the experience was not very good. There was no milk pool, red wine pool, or any special pool. In general, this package is cost-effective, and the hotel is also recommended. Just be careful with the hot springs.
